<script>

/* JACKPOT COUNTER */

let jackpot=128450000
const el=document.getElementById("jackpotValue")

setInterval(()=>{
jackpot+=Math.floor(Math.random()*9000)+2000
el.innerHTML="Rp "+jackpot.toLocaleString("id-ID")
